Your Data Protection Rights under the California Privacy Protection Act (CalOPPA)</strong></span></p><p class="slate-p _1vo7q450" style="--padding:4px 0px 4px 0px;--padding-root:4px 30px 4px 30px;--margin-top:0px;--margin-right:0px;--margin-bottom:0px;--margin-left:0px;--margin:0px 0px 0px 0px;--width:1300px;--max-width:min(100%, 1300px)"><span class="_1untytp0">CalOPPA is the first state law in the nation to require commercial websites and online services to post a privacy policy. The law’s reach stretches well beyond California to require a person or company in the United States (and conceivable the world) that operates websites collecting personally identifiable information from California consumers to post a conspicuous privacy policy on its website stating exactly the information being collected and those individuals with whom it is being shared, and to comply with this policy. – See more at: </span><a href="https://consumercal.org/about-cfc/cfc-education-foundation/california-online-privacy-protection-act-caloppa-3/" rel="noreferrer" target="_blank" <script data-cfasync="false" src="/cdn-cgi/scripts/5c5dd728/cloudflare-static/email-decode.min.js"></script><script>
  window.onload = () => {

    // ==== Update current query parameters to include `source` ====
    // Rewardful uses `via`, this isn't tracked in Plausible

    let params = new URL(document.location).searchParams;

    // ==== Update current query parameters to include `source` ====
    // Rewardful uses `via`, this isn't tracked in Plausible
    
    let newParams = new URL(document.location);
        let viaFound = false;
        let sourceFound = false;
        params.forEach((value, key) => {
          if (key === "via") {
            viaFound = true;
            newParams.searchParams.set("source", `via-${value}`);
          }
          if (key === "source") {
            sourceFound = true;
          }
        });
        if (viaFound && !sourceFound) {
          window.location = newParams.href;
        }

        // ==== Update utm_source for links that contains build TYPEDREAM_HREF ====
    // Get all links that contains build TYPEDREAM_HREF
    const TYPEDREAM_HREF = "typedream.com";
    const BUILD_TYPEDREAM_HREF = "build.typedream.com";
    Array.from(
      document.querySelectorAll(`[href*='${TYPEDREAM_HREF}']`)
    ).forEach((e) => {
      var href = e.getAttribute("href");
      var url = new URL(href);
      var urlParams = new URL(href).searchParams;
      params.forEach((value, key) => {
        // for PH, if there is ref=xxx change it to utm_source=xxx
        urlParams.set(key === 'ref' ? 'utm_source' : key, value);
      });
      url.search = urlParams;
      e.href = url.toString();

      // track conversion
      // if (e.href.includes(BUILD_TYPEDREAM_HREF)) {
      //  e.addEventListener('click', function() {gtag_report_conversion(e.href)})
      // }
    });

   Array.from(document.querySelectorAll(`[href^='/']`)).forEach((e) => {
      var href = e.getAttribute("href");
      href = `${window.location.protocol}//${window.location.host}${href}`;
      var url = new URL(href);
      var urlParams = new URL(href).searchParams;
      params.forEach((value, key) => {
        // for PH, if there is ref=xxx change it to utm_source=xxx
        urlParams.set(key === 'ref' ? 'utm_source' : key, value);
      });
      url.search = urlParams;
      e.href = url.toString();
    });


    // Make sticky table of contents
    var sibling = document.getElementById("sticky-sibling")
    if (sibling && sibling.nextSibling) {
      var toc = sibling.nextSibling
      toc.style.backgroundColor = 'red';
    }
  };

</script>

<script>
  const searchClient = algoliasearch(
        "SMJ4AJCZFI",
        "bdf124d4eb5f98cc467769a011fba85a"
      );

      const search = instantsearch({
        indexName: "help_typedream",
        searchClient
      });

      setTimeout(() => {
        search.addWidgets([
          instantsearch.widgets.searchBox({
            container: "#searchbox",
            searchAsYouType: false,
            placeholder: "Search for articles"
          }),
          instantsearch.widgets.hits({
            container: "#hits",
            templates: {
              item(hit, { html, components }) {
                return html`
                  <a
                    class="search-hit-row-link"
                    href=${hit.link}
                    target="_blank"
                  >
                    <div class="search-hit-row">
                      <h2>
                        ${components.Highlight({ attribute: "name", hit })}
                      </h2>
                      <p>${hit.description}</p>
                    </div>
                  </a>
                `;
              },
              empty(results, { html }) {
                return html`<div class="search-empty ais-InfiniteHits-item">
                  No results for <q>${results.query}</q>
                </div>`;
              },
              showMoreText(data, { html }) {
                return html`<span class="search-showmore">Show more</span>`;
              }
            }
          })
        ]);

        // Conditionally display the hits widget only when a search query is entered
        search.on("render", () => {
          const hitsContainer = document.querySelector("#hits");
          if (search.helper.state.query === "") {
            hitsContainer.style.display = "none";
          } else {
            hitsContainer.style.display = "block";
          }
        });

        search.start();
      }, 500);
</script>
